Error: Cannot open the page from the filesystem.
  • Chrome: Install SingleFileZ and enable the option "Allow access to file URLs" in the details page of the extension (chrome://extensions/?id=offkdfbbigofcgdokjemgjpdockaafjg).
  • Microsoft Edge: Install SingleFileZ and enable the option "Allow access to file URLs" in the details page of the extension (edge://extensions/?id=gofneaifncimeglaecpnanbnmnpfjekk).
  • Safari: Select "Disable Local File Restrictions" in the "Develop" menu.
Log in Sign up Home Public Questions Tags Users Companies Unanswered How do I hide an application by clicking the dock icon? Ask Question Asked 1 year, 1 month ago Modified 8 months ago Viewed 2k times This question shows research effort; it is useful and clear 1 This question does not show any research effort; it is unclear or not useful Save this question. Show activity on this post. Is it possible to configure the dock in such a way that a non-visible application becomes visible when the dock icon is clicked the first time and becomes invisible again when the dock icon is clicked a second time? I'm aware that with a long press and choosing Hide I can achieve what I want with just one click. applicationsdock Share Improve this question Follow Follow this question to receive notifications asked Feb 14, 2022 at 12:39 Michael S.Michael S. 39522 silver badges1515 bronze badges 3 3 Opt/click on switch to another app will hide the one your backgrounding. – Tetsujin Feb 14, 2022 at 13:41 Great. That is the answer. – Michael S. Feb 15, 2022 at 8:24 Let me throw that into the answer space - hopefully this time without autocorrect ruining my grammar ;)) – Tetsujin Feb 15, 2022 at 8:25 Add a comment  |  2 Answers 2 Sorted by: Reset to default Highest score (default) Date modified (newest first) Date created (oldest first) This answer is useful 5 This answer is not useful Save this answer. Show activity on this post. Opt/click on switching to another app will hide the one you're backgrounding. You can also do this by Opt/clicking any visible window of your new app. Share Improve this answer Follow Follow this answer to receive notifications answered Feb 15, 2022 at 8:26 TetsujinTetsujin 108k2525 gold badges182182 silver badges318318 bronze badges Add a comment  |  This answer is useful 1 This answer is not useful Save this answer. Show activity on this post. You can use DockAltTab or Dock Exposé for this. Plus then you also get window previews when hovering over dock icons.
